Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageWellTower partner Pegasus Senior Living contact form
URLhttps://www.pegasusseniorliving.com/contact/
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/23
Score1385
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1385, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 372. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 50. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 184

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 5 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 52 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package ibm, test IBMA_Color_Contrast_WCAG2AA, score 156 (Contrast ratio of text with background does not meet WCAG 2.1 AA)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R37, score 1 (Text has less than the minimum contrast)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 6 (Very low contrast)

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 73

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r83, score 4 (Overflow is hidden or clipped if the text is enlarged)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 69 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 64

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 36 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 3 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 46 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue contrastAAA

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 63

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r66, score 43 (Text contrast less than AAA requires)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast-enhanced, score 2 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Fail, score 41 (Text has insufficient contrast)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R76, score 1 (Text has less than the enhanced minimum contrast)

Issue labelBadID

WCAG: 1.3.1

Score: 60

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package ibm, test WCAG20_Label_RefValid, score 56 (for attribute does not reference a non-empty, unique id attribute of an input element)
  • Package wave, test a:label_orphaned, score 4 (Orphaned form label)

Issue duplicateID

WCAG: 4.1.1

Score: 33

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r3, score 16 (Element id attribute value is not unique)
  • Package axe, test duplicate-id-aria, score 4 (id attribute used in ARIA or in a label has a value that is not unique)
  • Package axe, test duplicate-id, score 1 (id attribute value is not unique)
  • Package continuum, test 94, score 16 (Element contains an id attribute set to a value that is not unique in the DOM)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_1.F77, score 8 (Duplicate id attribute value)
  • Package ibm, test RPT_Elem_UniqueId, score 8 (Element id attribute value is not unique within the document)
